Advantages:

Disadvantages:

posted:Posted April 15, 2024
msg:Fangcaodi is a parent-child hotel under the Delong Group. This one in Changxing opened early. According to my personal observation, except for the basic room type which is in the main building at the front desk, the others are single-family or townhouses, with single and double bedrooms. The room area is large, which is very suitable for a family or several families to travel together.
The hotel is located in a tea garden area. The hotel has its own tea garden, children's playground, indoor swimming pool (open in certain months), parent-child activities (picking tea, feeding animals, horseback riding, karting, DIY handicrafts, bonfire parties, etc.), and you can also rent electric vehicles for sightseeing. It is enough to walk the baby in the hotel for 1-2 days.

Facilities:
There is a disinfection cabinet in the room, so people can use the cups with confidence. This is worth a thumbs up~
There is a buffet restaurant and a Chinese restaurant, which are very close. At breakfast at 9:30 am on Sunday, there are so many people that they need to pick up the food in the buffet restaurant and then go to the Chinese restaurant for dinner. To be honest, the food is very average. I saw the waiter holding a large bag of bread and pouring it on the plate. . The hotel voucher contains only one meal worth 388 yuan. There are two tickets for staying for two nights, so the two meals are the same. This feeling is... . .
The location of the toilet roll next to the toilet in the bathroom is a bit disappointing. It is placed at the back, which is inconvenient to take. The quality of the roll is also a bit poor. It is easy to tear it apart with one hand. I hope it can be improved.

Hygiene:
After staying for two nights, the cleaning work on the second day was a bit delayed. It was almost 15 o'clock in the afternoon and it was not cleaned yet. I called it and it came. The cleaning lady said that they would be off work at 17 o'clock. . I can't help but wonder, if we don't call or call later, will someone clean it. . . (The auntie cleaned it very seriously)

Environment:
I have to mention that there are too many stink bugs in the room. . . And they all fell from the sky suddenly. Obviously the doors and windows were closed, there were about 6-8 in the room a day, which was frightening. .

Service:
Xiao Wang from the revenue depar**ent contacted and added WeChat in advance. He took good care of us during our stay. Thank you here~
The travel photography included in the hotel voucher is not recommended. The estimated shooting time was 60-90 minutes, but it was only 30 minutes in reality. Maybe the photographer saw that he was just shooting a little kid and didn't cooperate well, so he shot casually and his technique was not very good. The effect was similar to the portrait mode on iPhone, and the composition was even worse... It was a waste that we dressed up the kid. We have experienced travel photography in other hotels before, so it depends on the person.
